IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'

IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'
IF stomach_pain AND acidity AND ulcers_on_tongue AND vomiting AND cough AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'GERD'
IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'

IF itching AND skin_rash AND nodal_skin_eruptions AND dischromic__patches THEN diagnosis = 'Fungal infection'
IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'
IF stomach_pain AND acidity AND ulcers_on_tongue AND vomiting AND cough AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'GERD'
IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'

IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'
IF skin_rash AND chills AND joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND pain_behind_the_eyes AND back_pain AND malaise AND muscle_pain AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Dengue'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND constipation AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND toxic_look_(typhos) AND belly_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Typhoid'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'hepatitis A'
IF itching AND fatigue AND lethargy AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellow_urine AND yellowing_of_eyes AND malaise AND receiving_blood_transfusion AND receiving_unsterile_injections THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis B'
IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis D'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
IF continuous_sneezing AND chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND headache AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND throat_irritation AND redness_of_eyes AND sinus_pressure AND runny_nose AND congestion AND chest_pain AND loss_of_smell AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Common Cold'
IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'

IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis D'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
IF continuous_sneezing AND chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND headache AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND throat_irritation AND redness_of_eyes AND sinus_pressure AND runny_nose AND congestion AND chest_pain AND loss_of_smell AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Common Cold'
IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'

IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'
IF skin_rash AND joint_pain AND skin_peeling AND silver_like_dusting AND small_dents_in_nails AND inflammatory_nails THEN diagnosis = 'Psoriasis'
IF skin_rash AND high_fever AND blister AND red_sore_around_nose AND yellow_crust_ooze THEN diagnosis = 'Impetigo'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND nodal_skin_eruptions AND dischromic__patches THEN diagnosis = 'Fungal infection'
IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'
IF stomach_pain AND acidity AND ulcers_on_tongue AND vomiting AND cough AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'GERD'
IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'
IF skin_rash AND chills AND joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND pain_behind_the_eyes AND back_pain AND malaise AND muscle_pain AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Dengue'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND constipation AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND toxic_look_(typhos) AND belly_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Typhoid'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'hepatitis A'
IF itching AND fatigue AND lethargy AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellow_urine AND yellowing_of_eyes AND malaise AND receiving_blood_transfusion AND receiving_unsterile_injections THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis B'
IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'

IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'

IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '

IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '

IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'
IF skin_rash AND chills AND joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND pain_behind_the_eyes AND back_pain AND malaise AND muscle_pain AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Dengue'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND constipation AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND toxic_look_(typhos) AND belly_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Typhoid'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'hepatitis A'

IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'
IF skin_rash AND chills AND joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND pain_behind_the_eyes AND back_pain AND malaise AND muscle_pain AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Dengue'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND constipation AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND toxic_look_(typhos) AND belly_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Typhoid'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'hepatitis A'
IF itching AND fatigue AND lethargy AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellow_urine AND yellowing_of_eyes AND malaise AND receiving_blood_transfusion AND receiving_unsterile_injections THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis B'
IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis D'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
IF continuous_sneezing AND chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND headache AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND throat_irritation AND redness_of_eyes AND sinus_pressure AND runny_nose AND congestion AND chest_pain AND loss_of_smell AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Common Cold'
IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'
IF skin_rash AND joint_pain AND skin_peeling AND silver_like_dusting AND small_dents_in_nails AND inflammatory_nails THEN diagnosis = 'Psoriasis'

IF itching AND skin_rash AND nodal_skin_eruptions AND dischromic__patches THEN diagnosis = 'Fungal infection'

IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
IF continuous_sneezing AND chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND headache AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND throat_irritation AND redness_of_eyes AND sinus_pressure AND runny_nose AND congestion AND chest_pain AND loss_of_smell AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Common Cold'
IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'
IF skin_rash AND joint_pain AND skin_peeling AND silver_like_dusting AND small_dents_in_nails AND inflammatory_nails THEN diagnosis = 'Psoriasis'

IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'

IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '

IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'

IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'
IF stomach_pain AND acidity AND ulcers_on_tongue AND vomiting AND cough AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'GERD'
IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'

IF itching AND skin_rash AND nodal_skin_eruptions AND dischromic__patches THEN diagnosis = 'Fungal infection'
IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'
IF stomach_pain AND acidity AND ulcers_on_tongue AND vomiting AND cough AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'GERD'
IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'

IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'
IF skin_rash AND chills AND joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND pain_behind_the_eyes AND back_pain AND malaise AND muscle_pain AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Dengue'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND constipation AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND toxic_look_(typhos) AND belly_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Typhoid'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'hepatitis A'
IF itching AND fatigue AND lethargy AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellow_urine AND yellowing_of_eyes AND malaise AND receiving_blood_transfusion AND receiving_unsterile_injections THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis B'
IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis D'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
IF continuous_sneezing AND chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND headache AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND throat_irritation AND redness_of_eyes AND sinus_pressure AND runny_nose AND congestion AND chest_pain AND loss_of_smell AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Common Cold'
IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'

IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis D'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
IF continuous_sneezing AND chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND headache AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND throat_irritation AND redness_of_eyes AND sinus_pressure AND runny_nose AND congestion AND chest_pain AND loss_of_smell AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Common Cold'
IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'

IF chills AND fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND fast_heart_rate AND rusty_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Pneumonia'
IF constipation AND pain_during_bowel_movements AND pain_in_anal_region AND bloody_stool AND irritation_in_anus THEN diagnosis = 'Dimorphic hemmorhoids(piles)'
IF vomiting AND breathlessness AND sweating AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Heart attack'
IF fatigue AND cramps AND bruising AND obesity AND swollen_legs AND swollen_blood_vessels AND prominent_veins_on_calf THEN diagnosis = 'Varicose veins'
IF fatigue AND weight_gain AND cold_hands_and_feets AND mood_swings AND lethargy AND dizziness AND puffy_face_and_eyes AND enlarged_thyroid AND brittle_nails AND swollen_extremeties AND depression AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hypothyroidism'
IF fatigue AND mood_swings AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND sweating AND diarrhoea AND fast_heart_rate AND excessive_hunger AND muscle_weakness AND irritability AND abnormal_menstruation THEN diagnosis = 'Hyperthyroidism'
IF vomiting AND fatigue AND anxiety AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND drying_and_tingling_lips AND slurred_speech AND irritability AND palpitations THEN diagnosis = 'Hypoglycemia'
IF joint_pain AND neck_pain AND knee_pain AND hip_joint_pain AND swelling_joints AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Osteoarthristis'
IF muscle_weakness AND stiff_neck AND swelling_joints AND movement_stiffness AND painful_walking THEN diagnosis = 'Arthritis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND nausea AND spinning_movements AND loss_of_balance AND unsteadiness THEN diagnosis = '(vertigo) Paroymsal  Positional Vertigo'
IF skin_rash AND pus_filled_pimples AND blackheads AND scurring THEN diagnosis = 'Acne'
IF burning_micturition AND bladder_discomfort AND foul_smell_of_urine AND continuous_feel_of_urine THEN diagnosis = 'Urinary tract infection'
IF skin_rash AND joint_pain AND skin_peeling AND silver_like_dusting AND small_dents_in_nails AND inflammatory_nails THEN diagnosis = 'Psoriasis'
IF skin_rash AND high_fever AND blister AND red_sore_around_nose AND yellow_crust_ooze THEN diagnosis = 'Impetigo'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND nodal_skin_eruptions AND dischromic__patches THEN diagnosis = 'Fungal infection'
IF continuous_sneezing AND shivering AND chills AND watering_from_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Allergy'
IF stomach_pain AND acidity AND ulcers_on_tongue AND vomiting AND cough AND chest_pain THEN diagnosis = 'GERD'
IF itching AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Chronic cholestasis'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND stomach_pain AND burning_micturition AND spotting__urination THEN diagnosis = 'Drug Reaction'
IF vomiting AND indigestion AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND passage_of_gases AND internal_itching THEN diagnosis = 'Peptic ulcer diseae'
IF muscle_wasting AND patches_in_throat AND high_fever AND extra_marital_contacts THEN diagnosis = 'AIDS'
IF fatigue AND weight_loss AND restlessness AND lethargy AND irregular_sugar_level AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND obesity AND excessive_hunger AND increased_appetite AND polyuria THEN diagnosis = 'Diabetes '
IF vomiting AND sunken_eyes AND dehydration AND diarrhoea THEN diagnosis = 'Gastroenteritis'
IF fatigue AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND family_history AND mucoid_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Bronchial Asthma'
IF headache AND chest_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance AND lack_of_concentration THEN diagnosis = 'Hypertension '
IF acidity AND indigestion AND headache AND blurred_and_distorted_vision AND excessive_hunger AND stiff_neck AND depression AND irritability AND visual_disturbances THEN diagnosis = 'Migraine'
IF back_pain AND weakness_in_limbs AND neck_pain AND dizziness AND loss_of_balance THEN diagnosis = 'Cervical spondylosis'
IF vomiting AND headache AND weakness_of_one_body_side AND altered_sensorium THEN diagnosis = 'Paralysis (brain hemorrhage)'
IF itching AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND abdominal_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Jaundice'
IF chills AND vomiting AND high_fever AND sweating AND headache AND nausea AND diarrhoea AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Malaria'
IF itching AND skin_rash AND fatigue AND lethargy AND high_fever AND headache AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Chicken pox'
IF skin_rash AND chills AND joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND pain_behind_the_eyes AND back_pain AND malaise AND muscle_pain AND red_spots_over_body THEN diagnosis = 'Dengue'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND headache AND nausea AND constipation AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND toxic_look_(typhos) AND belly_pain THEN diagnosis = 'Typhoid'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND diarrhoea AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND muscle_pain THEN diagnosis = 'hepatitis A'
IF itching AND fatigue AND lethargy AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellow_urine AND yellowing_of_eyes AND malaise AND receiving_blood_transfusion AND receiving_unsterile_injections THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis B'
IF fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND yellowing_of_eyes AND family_history THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis C'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis D'
IF joint_pain AND vomiting AND fatigue AND high_fever AND yellowish_skin AND dark_urine AND nausea AND loss_of_appetite AND abdominal_pain AND yellowing_of_eyes AND acute_liver_failure AND coma AND stomach_bleeding THEN diagnosis = 'Hepatitis E'
IF vomiting AND yellowish_skin AND abdominal_pain AND swelling_of_stomach AND distention_of_abdomen AND history_of_alcohol_consumption AND fluid_overload THEN diagnosis = 'Alcoholic hepatitis'
IF chills AND vomiting AND fatigue AND weight_loss AND cough AND high_fever AND breathlessness AND sweating AND loss_of_appetite AND mild_fever AND yellowing_of_eyes AND swelled_lymph_nodes AND malaise AND phlegm AND chest_pain AND blood_in_sputum THEN diagnosis = 'Tuberculosis'
